 Votes were cast on Monday in the fifth phase of Jaipur Rural Lok Sabha seat in Rajasthan
 shantipurv sampann hue matdaan main jaipur (gramin) seat par 62
 While 02 per cent of the voting took place, Rajasthan has a total of 63 seats in 12 seats
 73 fisadi logon ne vot daale
 Eight candidates are in the fray for this seat in the 2019 Lok Sabha elections
 bhartiya janata party ne purv olympian or sena main adhikari rahe karnal rajyavardhan rathod ko tikat diya he jabaki congress ne krishna puniya ko pratyaashee banaaya he
 There is a direct contest between BJP and Congress on this seat
 baharhaal, rajasthan main donon hi partiyaan mishan 2019 ke liye target-25 kii ranneeti par kaam kar rahi hai
 But in the changed political equation after the assembly elections, it may be difficult for the BJP to repeat its previous performance in which it had won all the 25 seats of the state
 rajasthan main loksabhaa kii 25 siten hai
 The BJP, which won the last assembly election riding on the Modi wave, won all the seats in the Lok Sabha elections
 lekin 2018 main hue upachunaav main congress ne alvar or ajmer seat hathiyaa lee
 The Congress has returned to the state in the recent assembly elections, while the BJP is forced to sit in the opposition
 lihaaja 2014 main rajya main apane charam par rahi bijepi ke liye rajya main 2019 kii raah utani aasaan nahin he
 The situation is more or less similar in Jaipur Rural Lok Sabha seat as well
 saal 2008 ke parisemen main jaipur or alvar jile ke kuch hisson ko milakar jaipur gramin loksabhaa seat kaa gathan hua

 Lalchand Kataria is considered close to Congress veteran CP Joshi and should also be a minister of state in the UPA government
 saal 2014 main bhilwara kaa sameekaran gadabada jane ke baad kataaria ne yah seat seepi joshi ke ladane ke liye chhod di
 But the Congress could not save this seat in the Modi wave
 saal 2014 main bijepi ne is seat se purv olympian or sena main adhikari rahe karnal rajyavardhan rathod ko tikat dekar sabko chaunkaa diya
 Initially being a parachute candidate, Rathore also faced opposition from local BJP leaders Satish Poonia and Rao Rajendra Singh
 lekin modi lahar ke aage yah virodh kafoor ho gaya
 Rajyavardhan Singh Rathore defeated Congress veteran CP Joshi by a huge margin of 3,32,896 votes

 yah unke kul vetan kaa hissaa hota he

 kareeb 62 pratishat karmchaariyon kaa kahana tha ki kisi suvidha ke istemaal par bill dene kii prakriya kaaphi samay lene vaali hoti he

 kar laabh kii jatil or tamaam dastavej jutaney kii prakriya ko chalate kai karmchaaree to inase milane vaale kar laabh ko chhodana hi behatar samajhate hai

 iske liye unke vetan main eendhan, telephone bill, altie, gift vauchars aadi ko shaamil kiya jaataa he

 yah survey saat shaharon main 194 companiyon ke 1,233 karmchaariyon ke bich kiya gaya
 The survey revealed the fact that payment of telephone bills is the most popular tax benefit paid by companies to employees
 uske baad eendhan, altie or gagetts kaa number aata he
 About 62 percent of the employees said that the process of paying bills on the use of a facility is time consuming
 sirf ek bill daawey ke liye ausatan 23 minute kaa samay lagata he
 The comments survey main kaha gaya he ki 94 pratishat companiyaan abhi bhi kaaphi jatil or kagaji prakriyaaon kaa istemaal kar rahi hai

 There is talk of Manikarnika Ghat, the famous crematorium of Varanasi
 manyata he ki yahaan nrity karne vaali mahilaon ko agle janm main behatar jindagi milti he
 This is the reason that every year, women associated with prostitution from far and wide come here and decorate the festival
 is baar bhi buudhvaar kii raat nagarvadhuon ne puri raat jalati chitaaon ke bich nrity kar sadhana kii taaki agle janm main unhen apana sharir naa bechnaa pade
 It is said that this tradition has been going on here for many years
 samaaj kii tedi najaron kaa saamana karne vaali nagarvadhuon ne punya kamaane kii chahat main har saal kii tarah is baar bhi sadiyon se chali aa rahi parampara ko puri shiddat se nibhaayaa
 In addition to Varanasi, people from various cities including Chandauli, Mirzapur and Mumbai had come to the Mashan Baba Temple at the crematorium in Manikarnika
 unhone sabase pehle mandir main shmashaan nath baba kaa shringaar kiya
 After that she wandered all night in the stage adorned with burning pyres
 gauratlab he ki 16veen shatabdi main raja maan singh ne is mashaan nath mandir ko banwaaya tha
 There was such a tradition then that whenever the temple was built, after that there was a bhajan-kirtan
 lekin yahaan, shmashaan hone kii vajah se koi kalakar aane ko taiyaar nahin hua

 unhone ise sweekaar kar kiya
 She kept dancing all night in Baba's court and prayed that she should have a better life in the next life and not have to deal with her body for livelihood
 saal 2014-15 main rail durghatnaon main kul 292 logon ne apni jaan ganvaai he
 In the Rajya Sabha, Minister of Railways, Suresh Prabhu gave this information in written reply to a question
 unhone ek sawaal ke jawaab main rajyasabha ko bataaya ki 2014-15 main kul 135 badi durghatnaayen huin jinamein se 50 bina chaukeedaar vaale phatakon par or chah durghatnaayen chaukeedaar vaale phatakon par huin
 More than 150 people lost, Janaprabhu said that in 2014-15, 161 people died in accidents at railway gates
 unhone kaha ki is saal 11 november tak 69 durghatnaayen huyin jinamein 92 logon kii maut ho gayi
 According to the Railway Minister, several measures have been taken to prevent accidents at the gates
 in upayon main saamaajik jagakaruta ke lieesemembhiyaan shuru kiya janaa shaamil he
 The child will have to take the entire ticket to give a berth
 If you travel in the rail with your child up to 12 years, then you will have to buy his full ticket now
 darasal, railway ne bacchon ke half tikat lene par berth na dene kaa faisla kiya he
 According to railway rules, children from 5 years to 12 years are charged half the ticket
 abhi in bacchon ko arakshit shrenee main tikat book karaane par half tikat ke baavjood puri berth milti he
 But the railway has changed this rule from April 10 next year
 10 april 2016 se 5 saal se 12 saal ke bachche kaa half tikat lene par berth nahin mila karegi
 If you want a berth for the child, you will have to buy the entire ticket
 railway ke is faisle ko lekar kuch logon main naaraazgi he to kuch logon ne isko sahi bhi bataaya he
 In the case of infiltration of Pakistani soldiers and ruthless killing of two Indian soldiers, India has lodged a strong protest against Pakistan 
 videshmantri salmaan khurshid ne kaha he ki pakistan kaa hamalaa puri tarah se asweekaarya he or is tarah kii ghatnaon se dwipaksheeya sahyog ke jariye abhi tak hasil parinaamon par vipareet prabhaav padegaa
 Foreign Secretary Ranjan Mathai told Pakistani High Commissioner Salman Bashir that the Pakistan government should immediately investigate the incident, which is against international rules in every aspect
 videsh sachiv ne paak ucchayukta ko 27 disambar ko donon deshon ke bich hui us baithak kii yaad dilaai, jisamen aapasi bharosa badhaane or niyantran rekha kaa eemaandaaree se paalan karne kii baat hui thi
 However, Salman Bashir refused to comment on the matter
 jammu−kashmir main poonch ke mendhar sector main hui is ghatana se har bhartiya aakrosh main he, kyonki shahid hue ek jawan kaa shav kshat-vikshat haalat main mila he
 The Prime Minister has sought a full report on the shootout from the Ministry of External Affairs, the NSA and the Army Chief
 khabar he ki suraksha maamalon kii cabinet cameti kii baithak bhi bulaai ja sakati he
 Meanwhile, Defense Minister AK Antony termed it as an act of provocation and called it inhumane
 antni ne kaha he ki donon mulkon ke director general of military oparations yani dijiemo is mudde par baat karenge or bharat is ghatana ko lekar apni kadi aapatti darj karaayega
 BJP leader Arun Jaitley has described this action of Pakistan as provocative
 unhone kaha ki bharat sarkaar pakistan ke khilaaf sabooton ko saamne laakar duniya ke saamne use benakaab kare
 Significantly, in the Mendhar sector of Poonch in Jammu and Kashmir, Pakistani troops entered and attacked inside the Indian border on Tuesday
 48 ghante main duusari baar pakistan ne bina chetavanee ke golibari kii
 Taking advantage of the fog and haze, Pakistani soldiers crossed the Line of Control and then opened fire on Indian troops
 iske baad bhartiya javaanon ne bhi javaabi karrwai kii, lekin is puri golibari main do jawan shahid ho gaye
 According to sources, the body of a jawan was later found in a bad condition
 jawan kaa sir dhad se alag kiya hua tha
 The army is investigating how this condition of the dead body occurred
 isse pehle udi main niyantran rekha par hui jhadap kaa badla lene ke liye pakistan kii ore se karrwai kii gai
 The Indian government has strongly condemned the ceasefire violation from Pakistan
 raksha mantralay ke mutabik, sarkaar is ghatana ko uksaave kii karrwai maanate hue isaki ninda karti he
 According to the statement of Defense Ministry spokesman Satanshu Kar, after this incident the Director General of Military Operations of the two countries are in touch with each other and the government will take up the matter with the Government of Pakistan
 unke bayaan main bhi kaha gaya he ki pakistan kii ore se yudhviram ulanghan ke baad sarhad par sena alert ho gai he
 Earlier on Sunday morning, Pakistan also fired in the Uri sector
 is golabari main kai gharon ko bhi nuksaan pahunchaa, lekin us samay ulta pakistan ne bhartiya sena par aarope lagaaya ki usne seemaa paar kar uske jawan ko maar daalaa
 The comments udhar, javaanon kii maut ko lekar kargil yuddh ke shahid saurav kaaliya ke pita narendra kaaliya ne kaha he ki agar unke bete ke saath hue amanviya vyavhaar ko lekar koi karrwai hoti, to aaj yah naubat na aati
 According to him, Pakistan would not have dared to do so if some drastic steps were taken by India at that time
 iske saath hi unhone kaha ki pakistan pehle bhi aisi harakat kar chukaa he or ab bhi agar koi ection nahin liya gaya to vah aage bhi aisa karata rahegaa

 phalt ne kaha, ‘main is safal namakan ke liye bharat sarkaar, rajasthan sarkaar or jaipur shahar ko tahe dil se badhai detaa hum'ek varisht adhikari ne bataaya ki isioemoes (smarak or sthal par antarrashtriya parishad) ne 2018 main shahar kaa nirikshan kiya tha

 Protests against the film Padmavat continue in Bihar even after the Supreme Court verdict
 shanivaar ko sitamarhi main padmavat film ke pradarshan ke virodh main karani sena va hindu sanghathan se jude yuvakon ne shahar ke kiran chowk se paramparaagat hathiyaar (talwaar) se las yuvakon ne juluus nikaala
 The procession reached Cinema Road passing through the main road of the city
 julus main shaamil karani sena or hindu sanghathan se jude yuvakon ne padmavat film ke diarector ke virodh main pradarshan or narebaaji karte hue basushri cinema haul road pahunche
 Here the protesters demonstrated with a waving sword and a ruckus outside the Basushree Cinema Hall
 iske baad cinema chowk par sanjay lila bhansaali kaa putala dahan kiya
 After this, they performed outside all the cinema halls of the city and also used unparliamentary language against the director
 itnaa hi nahin, juluus main shaamil pradarshnkaree yuvakon ne haathon main talwaar liye hangaamaa karte shahar sthit aar-di pales ke sameep narebaaji karte hue cinema haul par patharbaji bhi kii, vahiin jila police ke kai jawan mook darshak bane updraviyon kii tasviir lete dikhe
 The Supreme Court has ruled out the release of the film everywhere denying any kind of ban on its performance, but first in Bihar, the Karni Sena in Muzaffarpur demonstrated against the film on the exact day the Supreme Court verdict came
 Was
 mujffarpur me supreme court ke aadesh ke baad karani sena ke lagbhag pachaas sadsy cinema haul parisar me talwaar or danda ke saath ghus gaye
 All the youths, holding open jeeps and dozens of motorcycles, carried swords and poles in their hands
 cinema haul parisar me ghuste hi un logon ne padmavat film ke poster ko haul ke andar se nikaal liya or baahar laakar naare lagaate hue poster ko faad diya

 philhal vah princeton uniwarsity main rachanaatmak lekhan kii professor hai
 The BSF officer of Kashmir is threatened by the terrorists
 saath hi unke parivaar ko bhi dhamkaaya ja rahaa he
 a Kashmiri youth posted as Assistant Commandant in BSF wrote a letter to Union Minister Maneka Gandhi complaining about it
 unhone apni bahan ko bhi dhamkee milane kaa daawa kiya
 The jawan said that after the murder of Lieutenant Omar Fayaz, he is concerned about the safety of his family
 menka gandhi ko likhaa patrambhshwa main assistant commandent ne bataaya ki chandigarh main unki bahan college hostel main rah rahi thi, lekin garmi kii chhuttiyon main duusari ladakiyon kii tarah use bhi college prashasan ne hostel chhodane ke liye kah diya
 She wrote a complaint to Women and Child Development Minister Maneka Gandhi on 14 May
 patr main unhone apni bahan hostel main rahane dene kii maang kii
 So that he does not have to go home
 unki bahan civil ejineering kii padhai kar rahi hai
 'danger to my family', Jawan said that he has demanded permission from the BSF officers to carry arms with him on leave
 unhone kaha, 'khaastaur par aatankwaad prabhavit ilaakon main rahane vaale javaanon ko hathiyaar le jane kii anumati di jaae
 The jawan told that he has to go home to Jammu for his relative's wedding in the next two months
 'mere or mere parivaar ke sadasyon ko hameshaa aatankwaadiyon se dhamkee milti rahati hai
 After the murder of Lieutenant Omar Fayaz, i am concerned about the safety of my family
 meri maa jammu main akeli rahati hai, jabaki meri bahan chandigarh main he
 i am worried now because terrorists are targeting our families
 'kashmiriyon ke liye chintitis jawan ye bhi kaha ki wo ab un sabhi kashmiriyon ke liye chintit hai jo sena yaa ardhasanya balon main sevarat hai
 He said, 'despite opposition, we joined the army and now the practice of killing Kashmiri jawans is like hanging a sword on us
 menka gandhi ne kii madadakendriya mantri menka gandhi ne bataaya ki unhen ek mail ke jariye ye shikaayat mili thi
